<Heading
  as={"h1"}
  className={"openapi__heading"}
  children={"Resume an agent turn with executed tool call responses."}
>
</Heading>

<MethodEndpoint
  method={"post"}
  path={"/v1alpha/agents/{agent_id}/session/{session_id}/turn/{turn_id}/resume"}
  context={"endpoint"}
>
  
</MethodEndpoint>



Resume an agent turn with executed tool call responses.
When a Turn has the status `awaiting_input` due to pending input from client side tool calls, this endpoint can be used to submit the outputs from the tool calls once they are ready.

<Heading
  id={"request"}
  as={"h2"}
  className={"openapi-tabs__heading"}
  children={"Request"}
>
</Heading>

<ParamsDetails
  parameters={[{"name":"agent_id","in":"path","description":"The ID of the agent to resume.","required":true,"schema":{"type":"string"}},{"name":"session_id","in":"path","description":"The ID of the session to resume.","required":true,"schema":{"type":"string"}},{"name":"turn_id","in":"path","description":"The ID of the turn to resume.","required":true,"schema":{"type":"string"}}]}
>
  
</ParamsDetails>
